## Case: 1957
| Case | Setup | Description |
| ---- | ----- | ----------- |
| **1957** | **L U' R L U L' B' R'** | **([0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0], [0, 0, 1, 2], [2, 4, 0, 3, 1, 5])** |
